	{
	/* $('input:radio[name=format]:checked').val();*/

	test=0;

			ready_copy=1;
			test=1;
 
			}       
		});
     }
	 if(IsNumeric(surahno)==false || IsNumeric(ayahno)==false || !surahno || !ayahno)
	 {
	
			  $('#text-to-copy').text('');
			  str="";

	 }
 str=ayahno;
 strs=surahno;
 }

<script>

function open_div(id)
{
	if(id==1)
	{
		$("a.z-test").width("0px");
		$(".zclip").width("0px");
		$("#ZeroClipboardMovie_1").width("0px");
		document.getElementById('search-alim').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('goto-quran').style.display  = 'none';
		document.getElementById('goto-hadith').style.display = 'none';
		$('.top-block').attr('id', 'searchalim');
		$("#sral").addClass("current");
		$("#goqu").removeClass("current");
		$("#goha").removeClass("current");
		
	}
	else if(id==2)
	{
		$("a.z-test").width("67px");
		$(".zclip").width("67px");
		$("#ZeroClipboardMovie_1").width("67px");

		document.getElementById('search-alim').style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById('goto-quran').style.display  = 'block';
		document.getElementById('goto-hadith').style.display = 'none';
		$('.top-block').attr('id', 'gotoquran');
		$("#goqu").addClass("current");
		$("#sral").removeClass("current");
		$("#goha").removeClass("current");
	}
	else if(id==3)
	{
		$("a.z-test").width("0px");
		$(".zclip").width("0px");
		$("#ZeroClipboardMovie_1").width("0px");
		document.getElementById('search-alim').style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById('goto-quran').style.display  = 'none';
		document.getElementById('goto-hadith').style.display = 'block';
		$('.top-block').attr('id', 'gotohadith');
		$("#goha").addClass("current");
		$("#sral").removeClass("current");
		$("#goqu").removeClass("current");
	}
}
// Remove from drop down
function RemoveItemInList(id)
    {
        var list  = document.getElementById(id);
        if(list.options.length > 0)
        {
            for(var i = list.options.length - 1; i >= 0; i--)
            {
                 list.remove(i);
            }
        }
        else
        {
           alert('Unable to remove. List is Empty!');
        }
    }

//Find array object
function array_find(arr,obj) {
  a=0;
   for (key in arr)
   {
     arrlower = arr[key].toLowerCase();
	 objlower = obj.toLowerCase(); 
	 if(arrlower==objlower)
	 {
	   a=1;
	   return key;
	 
	  }
   }
   
  if(a==0)
   return false;
}


function IsNumeric(strString)
   //  check for valid numeric strings	
   {
   var strValidChars = "0123456789";
   var strChar;
   var blnResult = true;

   if (strString.length == 0) return false;

   //  test strString consists of valid characters listed above
   for (i = 0; i < strString.length && blnResult == true; i++)
      {
      strChar = strString.charAt(i);
      if (strValidChars.indexOf(strChar) == -1)
         {
         blnResult = false;
         }
      }
   return blnResult;
   }

	 txt_values = quran_txt.split(":");
	 surahno=txt_values[0];
	 //alert("surahno"+txt_values[0]+"ayahno"+txt_values[1]);
		 if(array_find(arr_surahname,surahno)!=false)
		 {
		  surahno = array_find(arr_surahname,surahno);
		  validate = 1;
		 }
		 else
		 {
			 if(IsNumeric(surahno)==false)
			 {
			   document.getElementById('quran_txt').value="Surah:Ayah";
			   alert("Invalid value for Surah.");
			   return false;
			 }
			 else if(surahno<1 || surahno>114)
			 {
			    document.getElementById('quran_txt').value="Surah:Ayah";
				alert("Invalid value for Surah.");
			    return false;
			 }
		 }
		 
		 if(quran_txt.search(":")!=-1)
          ayahno=txt_values[1];
		 else
		  ayahno=1; 
		  
		  if(parseInt(ayah[surahno])<parseInt(ayahno) || parseInt(ayahno)<=0)
		  {
		     document.getElementById('quran_txt').value="Surah:Ayah";
			 alert("Invalid value for Ayah.");
			 return false;
		  }
  }	

    if(ayahno=="")
	 {
		ayahno  = 1;
	 }

 arr_pageno['108-1'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['107-6'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['107-4'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['107-2'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['106-4'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['106-2'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['108-2'] = '602'; 
 arr_pageno['111-3'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['111-1'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['110-2'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['109-6'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['109-4'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['109-2'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['111-4'] = '603'; 
 arr_pageno['111-2'] = '603';

 arr_pageno['114-5'] = '604';

 arr_pageno['114-1'] = '604'; 
 arr_pageno['113-4'] = '604'; 
 arr_pageno['113-2'] = '604'; 
 arr_pageno['112-4'] = '604'; 
 arr_pageno['112-2'] = '604'; 
  var pageno =  arr_pageno[surahno+"-"+ayahno];
  
  if(type=='trans')
  {
	window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/quran/ayah/compare/"+surahno+"/"+ayahno;
  }
  else if(type=='arabic')
  {
    window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/quran/surah/arabic/"+surahno+"/ARB#"+ayahno;
  }
  else if(type=='calli')
  {
    window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/quran/page/arabic/"+surahno+"/"+pageno+"/"+ayahno;
  }
  else if(type=='tafsir')
  {
  
t = 'http://www.alim.org/alim/go/ayah?go='+ayahno+'&sura='+surahno+'&code='+'TIK';
		var vhr = $.ajax({         
			url: t,
			dataType: 'json' ,
			success: function(data) { 

  window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/quran/AlQuran-tafsir/TIK/"+surahno+"/"+data.data;
}
});
            

  }
  
}

function hadith_select(codeid)
{
  volume_cnt = new Array(); 
 volume_cnt['AMH'] = '61'; 
 volume_cnt['SHB'] = '9'; 
 volume_cnt['FQS'] = '5'; 
   number_count = new Array(); 
 number_count['SHB_1'] = '832'; 
 number_count['SHB_2'] = '823'; 
 number_count['SHB_3'] = '895'; 
 number_count['SHB_4'] = '841';

 number_count['AMH_15'] = '50'; 
 number_count['AMH_16'] = '58'; 
 number_count['AMH_17'] = '58'; 
 number_count['AMH_18'] = '60'; 
 number_count['AMH_19'] = '17'; 
 number_count['AMH_20'] = '264'; 
 number_count['AMH_21'] = '51'; 
 number_count['AMH_22'] = '17'; 
 number_count['AMH_23'] = '13'; 
 number_count['AMH_24'] = '9'; 
 number_count['AMH_25'] = '19'; 
 number_count['AMH_26'] = '7'; 
 number_count['AMH_27'] = '16'; 
 number_count['AMH_28'] = '57'; 
 number_count['AMH_29'] = '109'; 
 number_count['AMH_30'] = '17'; 
 number_count['AMH_31'] = '102'; 
 number_count['AMH_32'] = '16'; 
 number_count['AMH_33'] = '3'; 
 number_count['AMH_34'] = '5'; 
 number_count['AMH_35'] = '4'; 
 number_count['AMH_36'] = '54'; 
 number_count['AMH_37'] = '9'; 
 number_count['AMH_38'] = '25'; 
 number_count['AMH_39'] = '15'; 
 number_count['AMH_40'] = '8'; 
 number_count['AMH_41'] = '35'; 
 number_count['AMH_42'] = '15'; 
 number_count['AMH_43'] = '15'; 
 number_count['AMH_44'] = '2'; 
 number_count['AMH_45'] = '26'; 
 number_count['AMH_46'] = '10'; 
 number_count['AMH_47'] = '18'; 
 number_count['AMH_48'] = '19'; 
 number_count['AMH_49'] = '39'; 
 number_count['AMH_50'] = '18'; 
 number_count['AMH_51'] = '16'; 
 number_count['AMH_52'] = '7'; 
 number_count['AMH_53'] = '8'; 
 number_count['AMH_54'] = '44'; 
 number_count['AMH_55'] = '3'; 
 number_count['AMH_56'] = '28'; 
 number_count['AMH_57'] = '2'; 
 number_count['AMH_58'] = '15'; 
 number_count['AMH_59'] = '1'; 
 number_count['AMH_60'] = '1'; 
 number_count['AMH_61'] = '1'; 
 number_count['HDQ_1'] = '40'; 
 number_count['SAD_1'] = '2517'; 
 number_count['SHM_1'] = '1415'; 
 number_count['TIR_1'] = '1691'; 
 number_count['FQS_1'] = '164'; 
 number_count['FQS_2'] = '154'; 
 number_count['FQS_3'] = '156'; 
 number_count['FQS_4'] = '149'; 
 number_count['FQS_5'] = '136'; 
   
     var volcount = "";
     var x = document.getElementById('hd_vol');
     RemoveItemInList('hd_vol');

       if(volume_cnt[codeid])
        volcount = volume_cnt[codeid];
		
	   if(volcount=="")
	   {
	   	 var y = document.createElement('option');
            y.text = "Volume of Hadith";
            y.value = "";
            try {
                x.add(y);
            }
            catch(ex) {
                x.add(y,null);
            }
	   }
	   else
	   {
		   for(i=1;i<=volcount;i++) {
			    
				if(codeid=='FQS')
				 var display = "Volume "+i+" of Fiqh";
				else
				 var display = "Volume "+i+" of Hadith";
				 
				var option  = i;
	
				var y = document.createElement('option');
				y.text = display;
				y.value = option;

				try {
					x.add(y);
				}
				catch(ex) {
					x.add(y,null);
				}
		  }
	   }
	   
	   
	   var num_count = "";
	   var a = document.getElementById('hd_no');
         RemoveItemInList('hd_no');
       
	   var numid = codeid+'_1';
       if(number_count[numid])
        num_count = number_count[numid];
		
	   if(num_count=="")
	   {
	   	    var b   = document.createElement('option');
            b.text  = "Hadith Number";
            b.value = "";
            try {
                a.add(b);
            }
            catch(ex) {
                a.add(b,null);
            }
	   }
	   else
	   {
		   for(i=1;i<=num_count;i++) {
			
				var display = "Number "+i;
				var option  = i;
	
				var b   = document.createElement('option');
				b.text  = display;
				b.value = option;

				try {
					a.add(b);
				}
				catch(ex) {
					a.add(b,null);
				}
		  }
	   }
 
}

function gotohadith()
{
  var hd_book = document.getElementById('hd_book').value;
  var hd_vol  = document.getElementById('hd_vol').value;
  var hd_no   = document.getElementById('hd_no').value;
  if(hd_book=="" || hd_book=='Book of Hadith')
  {
  	alert("Select Hadith Book.");
	return false;
  }
  if(hd_book=='SAD' || hd_book=='HDQ' || hd_book=='TIR' || hd_book=='SHM')
  {
  	window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/hadith/"+hd_book+"/"+hd_no;
  }
  else if(hd_book=='AMH' || hd_book=='SHB')
  {
    window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/hadith/"+hd_book+"/"+hd_no+"/"+hd_vol;
  }
  else if(hd_book=='FQS')
  {
     window.location = "http://www.alim.org/library/hadith/fiq/"+hd_book+"/"+hd_vol+"/"+hd_no;
  }
  
}
function select_text()
{

 RemoveItemInList('ayah_no');
 var x  = document.getElementById('ayah_no');
 var x1 = document.getElementById('surah');
 var x2 = document.getElementById('juz_no');
 var y = document.createElement('option');
            y.text = "Ayah";
            y.value = "";
            try {
                x.add(y);
            }
            catch(ex) {
                x.add(y,null);
            }
		x1.selectedIndex =0;
		x2.selectedIndex =0;
			
}

function select_surah()
{
 	document.getElementById('quran_txt').value = "Surah:Ayah";
	var x2 = document.getElementById('juz_no');
	x2.selectedIndex =0;
}
function select_juz()
{
 	document.getElementById('quran_txt').value = "Surah:Ayah";
	var x2 = document.getElementById('surah');
	x2.selectedIndex =0;
	RemoveItemInList('ayah_no');
	var x  = document.getElementById('ayah_no');
	var y = document.createElement('option');
            y.text = "Ayah";
            y.value = "";
            try {
                x.add(y);
            }
            catch(ex) {
                x.add(y,null);
            }
}


function checkKeycode(e) {
var keycode;
if (window.event) keycode = window.event.keyCode;
else if (e) keycode = e.which;
if(keycode==13)
{
gotopage('trans');
}
}

<td height="30" align="left" valign="top" class="form"><textarea class="form-textarea" id="edit-message-content" name="message_content">Assalam-u-alaikum. I ran across this new site, called Alim.org, where they have the complete and fully searchable text of multiple Quran translations, Hadith, Fiqh, and many other classical sources of Islamic knowledge. But whats interesting is that they have a unique feature that I havent seen anywhere before: every Ayah of the Quran, each Hadith, page of Fiqh, etc. can have discussions, comments, and voting associated with it.
	
	What I like about it is that it's not just a one-way "read-only" site that simply puts books online; they have really taken Web 2.0 and social networking and applied to the most important part of a Muslim's life: Qur'an and Hadith.
	
	If you haven't seen it, check it out at http://www.alim.org. By the way, it's run by a non-profit foundation so if you like what you see you should click the "donate" button and give some money, too.</textarea></td>

			$('.noayah').show();

<div class="content"><script language="javascript">
function setCookieJav()
{
	var exdate=new Date();
	var exdays = 1;
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
	value = "a";
	var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
	document.cookie="rem_notebook=" + c_value;
}
</script>

<script async>
	function getCookiesort(c_name)
{
	if (document.cookie.length>0)
	{
		c_start=document.cookie.indexOf(c_name + "=");
		if (c_start!=-1)
		{
			c_start=c_start + c_name.length+1;
			c_end=document.cookie.indexOf(";",c_start);
			if (c_end==-1) c_end=document.cookie.length;
			return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start,c_end));
		}
	}
	return "";
}
	cookieval = getCookiesort('anonymformat')-1;
	if(cookieval);
	{
	$('input[name=format]:radio').each(function(){
	   $('input[name=format]:radio:eq('+cookieval+')').attr('checked', true);  
	  });
	}
	</script>
<script async>
	function enable_range_edit()
	{
	
	jQuery('.update-copy').html('<img class="copy-img" src="http://www.alim.org/sites/all/themes/alim/images/goto-copy-icon.png" width:"37" height="37" border="0" />');
	jQuery('.update-copy').hide();
	jQuery('.update-copy').hide();
	jQuery('.range-edit').show();
	}
	$('#copy-close').click(function() {
	jQuery('.range-edit').hide();
	jQuery('.copy_range').hide();
	jQuery('.noayah').hide();
	jQuery('.update-copy').html('');
	jQuery('.range_copied').hide();
	});
	jQuery(".copy_range").mouseup(function() {
					return false;
				});
	if($.browser.mozilla)
	{
	jQuery(".zclip").mouseup(function() {
					return false;
				});
	}
/*	$(document).click(function(e) {
	if($(e.target).parent("a.z-test").length==0) {

	jQuery('.noayah').hide();
	jQuery('.range_copied').hide();

	});*/
	
	jQuery('a.z-test').click(function() {
	if(test==1)
	{
	jQuery('.copy_range').show();
	jQuery('.copy_range_top').show();
	jQuery('.copy_range_mid').show();
	jQuery('.copy_range_bottom').show();
	}
	});
	
	jQuery('.update-copy').click(function() {
	jQuery('.update-copy').html('');
	jQuery('.range-edit').hide();
	jQuery('.copied').hide();
	jQuery('.range_copied').show();
	
	});
	</script>

            var problemVal = jQuery("#problem").is(":checked");

            if (problemVal == true) {
                jQuery(".problemSection").show();
            } else {
                jQuery(".problemSection").hide();
            }
            jQuery("#problem").change(function() {
                var problemVal = jQuery("#problem").is(":checked");

                if (problemVal == true) {
                    jQuery(".problemSection").show();
                } else {
                    jQuery(".problemSection").hide();
                }

                var statisticVal = jQuery("#statisticsStat").is(":checked");

                if (problemVal == true || statisticVal == true) {

                    jQuery(".commonSection").show();
                } else {

                    jQuery(".commonSection").hide();
                }


            });
            var statisticVal = jQuery("#statisticsStat").is(":checked");
            if (statisticVal == true) {
                jQuery(".statisticsSection").show();
                var SlowQuerysel = jQuery("#SlowQuery").is(":checked");

             

                if (SlowQuerysel == true) {
                    jQuery(".form-item-query-time-limit").show();
                } else {
                    jQuery(".form-item-query-time-limit").hide();
                }
            } else {
                jQuery(".statisticsSection").hide();
            }

                } else {

<div class=" ">
<div class="well aboutus">
<span class="head-bg span12"> <h2> Learn Quran And Hadith with Alim's Unique Platform</h2> </span>
You had always wished a great Islamic program and you had it on your fingertips since 1991 on a CD-ROM and since 2010 online. It was then Alim and now Alim.org a wonderful platform for you to study and enhance your knowledge of the Quran and other authentic Islamic content. At Alim Foundation, we are passionate about giving you the Quran translations, Quran recitations (Listen Quran Online), authentic <a href="http://www.alim.org/library/hadith/SAD/1">ahadith</a> (Abu-Dawood, An-Nawawi, Al-Muwatta, Al-Qudsi, Al-Tirmidhi, Fiqh-us-Sunnah, Sahih Al-Bukhari and Sahih Muslim), Islamic <a href="http://www.alim.org/library/references/dictionary/a">references</a> and the <a href="http://www.alim.org/library/history/timeline/6th%20Century%20(500-599)%20C.E.">history of Islam</a>, <a href="http://www.alim.org/library/biography/stories/SOP">Stories of the Prophets</a>, history of Khulfae Rashidun and more. Alim.org includes <a href="http://www.alim.org/library/quran/surah/english/1/ASD">Quran translations</a> of Asad, Yusuf Ali, Pickthall and Malik. The website incorporated the same high-quality content that was available in the CD-ROM version plus an online social network platform for Muslims who care about Islamic knowledge. Furthermore, we've added tools for research, studying, teaching, discussion, and Quranic memorization and reading. Explore the site and discover the world's most useful Islamic software!
</div>
</div>
<div class=" ">
<div class="well unique-platform">
<span class="head-bg span12"> <h2> About Us</h2> </span>
<div id="block-views-splash_about_us-block_1" class="clear-block block block-views">
<div class="content"><div class="view view-splash-about-us view-id-splash_about_us view-display-id-block_1 view-dom-id-1">
<div class="view-content">
<div class="views-row views-row-1 views-row-odd views-row-first views-row-last">
<div class="heading_div"><h2>About US</h2></div>
<div class="about-us">
This site is brought to you by the same brothers and sisters that created The Alim CD-ROM software for Windows. Here you will find all the same high quality content that was available in the CD-ROM version plus an online social network for Muslims who care about Islamic knowledge. Furthermore, we've added tools for research, studying, teaching, discussion, and Qur'anic memorization and reading. Explore the site and discover the world's most useful Islamic software! </div>
</div>
</div>
</div> </div>

<script async>
  $("ul.nice-menu-down").prepend('<li id="menu-3513" ><a href=""></a></li>');
  $(document).ready(function() {
 $("#mailing-list-subscription-form-1")[0].reset();
  	var insert_success = 0;						   
$('#mailing-list-subscription-form-1 #edit-submit-1').click(function(e) {
		 if($('#edit-mail-wrapper input').val() && $('#edit-mail-wrapper input').val()!=" " && $('#edit-name-wrapper input').val()!=" " ){ 
		  $('#block-mailing_list-1 h2').append('<span class="inserting_status" style="color:red;font-size: 18px;"> Subscription in Process..</span>');																 
		 var email_id = $('#edit-mail-wrapper input').val();
		 var name = $('#edit-name').val();
		 
			  jQuery.ajax({
					url: '/alim/custom/php_list/subscribe?mail_id='+email_id+'&name='+name,
					type:'POST',
					async: false,
					dataType: 'text/html',
					success: function(data) {
						insert_success = 1;
						console.log(data.data);
						},
					error:function() {
						
						insert_success = 2;
					 }
											 
				}).ajaxComplete(function(){});
}
else 
{
	if(insert_success ==0 )
	{
		alert("Please enter a valid Email id and Name");
		return false;
		inserting_status = 0;
	}
}


});
  
	$('.marquee0 div:eq(0)').addClass('marquee11');
	$('.marquee0 .marquee11 div:eq(0)').addClass('marq_child');

	$('.marq_child').css('top',-5);
 });
	</script>
<script type="text/javascript" async>
	window.onload=function() {
	var plend = new Date();
	var plload = plend.getTime() - plstart.getTime();
	if(plload<1000)
	lc = "Very Fast";
	else if (plload<2000)
	lc = "Fast";
	else if (plload<3000)
	lc = "Medium";
	else if (plload<5000)
	lc = "Sluggish";
	else if (plload<10000)
	lc = "Slow";
	else
	lc="Very Slow";
	var fn = window.location.href;
	//if( document.location.search)
	//fn += document.location.search;
	try {
  ga('send', 'event', {
    eventCategory: 'Page Load (ms)',
    eventAction: lc + ' Loading Pages',
	eventLabel: fn,
	eventValue : plload,
    transport: 'beacon'
  });
	
	
	} catch(err){}
	}
	</script>
<script async>
	//Copy to clipboard flash object positioning
	$(window).resize(function() {
		var left= $('.copy_btn').position().left;
		var top = $('.copy_btn').position().top;
		var right=$('.copy_btn').position().right;
		var window_width=$(window).width();
		$("#zclip-ZeroClipboardMovie_1").css('left',left);
		$("#zclip-ZeroClipboardMovie_1").css('top',top);
		$(".z-test").css('left',left);
		$(".z-test").css('right','0');
		$(".z-test").css('top',top);
		$(".copy_range").css('top',top+30);
		var left1=left-198;
		if(window_width+17==980)
			left1=left-100;
		//$(".copy_range").css('left',left1);
		/*$(".copy_range").css('right','0');*/
		$(".loading_round").css('top',top);
		$(".loading_round").css('left',left);
		$(".loading_round").css('right','0');
     });
	 $(window).load(function() {
	 	var left= $('.copy_btn').position().left;
		var top = $('.copy_btn').position().top;
		var right=$('.copy_btn').position().right;
		var window_width=$(window).width();

		$("#zclip-ZeroClipboardMovie_1").css('left',left);
		$("#zclip-ZeroClipboardMovie_1").css('top',top);
		$(".z-test").css('left',left);
		$(".z-test").css('right','0');
		$(".z-test").css('top',top);
		$(".copy_range").css('top',top+30);
		var left1=left-198;
		if(window_width+17==980)
			left1=left-100;
		//$(".copy_range").css('left',left1);
		/*$(".copy_range").css('right','0');*/
		$(".loading_round").css('top',top);
		$(".loading_round").css('left','0');
		$(".loading_round").css('right',right);
	  });
	</script>
